    <script type="rocketlazyloadscript">
        function mutSetCookie(value){
            // Set cookie for 1 year
            var date = new Date();
            date.setTime(date.getTime() + (365*24*60*60*1000)); // 365 days
            document.cookie = "mut_cookie_consent=" + value + "; expires=" + date.toUTCString() + "; path=/; SameSite=Lax";
            
            // Immediately remove notice
            var el = document.getElementById('mut-cookie');
            if(el){ el.remove(); }
        }
    </script>

    <script type="rocketlazyloadscript">
        function mutSetCookie(value){
            // Set cookie for 1 year
            var date = new Date();
            date.setTime(date.getTime() + (365*24*60*60*1000)); // 365 days
            document.cookie = "mut_cookie_consent=" + value + "; expires=" + date.toUTCString() + "; path=/; SameSite=Lax";
            
            // Immediately remove notice
            var el = document.getElementById('mut-cookie');
            if(el){ el.remove(); }
        }
    </script>
